\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01211}01211\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}measure=True\`{}\`{}\ to\ find\ the\ fastest\ method\ by\ timing\ the\ convolution.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01217}01217\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ function.\ These\ experiments\ measured\ the\ ratio\ between\ the\ time\ required}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01218}01218\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ when\ using\ \`{}\`{}method='auto'\`{}\`{}\ and\ the\ time\ required\ for\ the\ fastest\ method}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01219}01219\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ (i.e.,\ \`{}\`{}ratio\ =\ time\_auto\ /\ min(time\_fft,\ time\_direct)\`{}\`{}).\ In\ these}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01220}01220\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ experiments,\ we\ found:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01221}01221\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01222}01222\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ *\ There\ is\ a\ 95\%\ chance\ of\ this\ ratio\ being\ less\ than\ 1.5\ for\ 1D\ signals}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01223}01223\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ and\ a\ 99\%\ chance\ of\ being\ less\ than\ 2.5\ for\ 2D\ signals.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01224}01224\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ *\ The\ ratio\ was\ always\ less\ than\ 2.5/5\ for\ 1D/2D\ signals\ respectively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01225}01225\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ *\ This\ function\ is\ most\ inaccurate\ for\ 1D\ convolutions\ that\ take\ between\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01226}01226\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ and\ 10\ milliseconds\ with\ \`{}\`{}method='direct'\`{}\`{}.\ A\ good\ proxy\ for\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01227}01227\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ (at\ least\ in\ our\ experiments)\ is\ \`{}\`{}1e6\ <=\ in1.size\ *\ in2.size\ <=\ 1e7\`{}\`{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01228}01228\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01229}01229\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ The\ 2D\ results\ almost\ certainly\ generalize\ to\ 3D/4D/etc\ because\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01230}01230\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ implementation\ is\ the\ same\ (the\ 1D\ implementation\ is\ different).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01231}01231\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01232}01232\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ All\ the\ numbers\ above\ are\ specific\ to\ the\ EC2\ machine.\ However,\ we\ did\ find}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01233}01233\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ that\ this\ function\ generalizes\ fairly\ decently\ across\ hardware.\ The\ speed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01234}01234\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ tests\ were\ of\ similar\ quality\ (and\ even\ slightly\ better)\ than\ the\ same}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01235}01235\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ tests\ performed\ on\ the\ machine\ to\ tune\ this\ function's\ numbers\ (a\ mid-\/2014}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__signaltools_8py_source_l01236}01236\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ 15-\/inch\ MacBook\ Pro\ with\ 16GB\ RAM\ and\ a\ 2.5GHz\ Intel\ i7\ processor).}}
